Also, the court had asked that why should they be heard in this case? The Supreme Court also questioned the CBI as to why the agency did not file an appeal even after 12 years of the Delhi High Court acquitting the accused
 On 31 May 2005, the Delhi High Court discharged the three Hinduja brothers and the Bofors Company
 supreme court main ek or ahm mukadmaa jalikattu parampara ko lekar he

 agar aisa he to court is maamle ko sanvaidhanik bench ke samaksh bhejega

 The date of March 14 in history is something special for the history of science
 is din saapekshata kaa siddhant (theory of relativity) or dravyaman evam urja kaa sambandh bataane vaale mahaan vaigyanik albert oinstin kaa janm hua tha
 At the same time, the second great scientist who reshaped space physics, Stephen Hawking died on this date
 haking ne sirf wheelchair par baithe-baithe hi kwantum gravity or brahmand vigyaan kaa adhyayan kiya or albert oinstin ke baad duniya ke sabase mahaan saidhantik bhautikeevid bane
 Apart from these two events, this day has been witness to many more important events
 1883: mahaan arthshaastri karl marks kaa nidhan
 1905: Birth of French sociologist, philosopher and journalist Raymond Aarons
 1913 : malayalam lekhak shankaran kutti pottaccat kaa janm
 1931: First spoken Indian film 'alamara' was screened
 1939: slovakia ne aazaadee kii ghoshnaa kii
 1963: Death of famous freedom fighter and Chief Minister of Rajasthan Jayanarayan Vyas
 1965: prasiddh bhartiya film abhinayta aamir khan kaa janm
 1998: Sonia Gandhi becomes the President of the Indian National Congress
 2013: shi chinaping ne china kii bagdor sanbhali

 isaki sabase zyada maarmadhyam vargke pariwaron par padegi

 cancer se ubar rahe bhartiya cricketer yuvaraj singh ko ummid he ki vah sitambar main hone vaali vishwa twanti-20 championships se maidan par vaapasi karne main safal rahenge, haalanki vah ise khud ke liye 'badi chunauti' maanate hai

 keval cancer kaa marij hi samaj saktaa he ki vah kis dasha se gujara he
 So it will be a big challenge for me to come back and play for India again
 baayen haath ke is ballebaaj ne sidhe taur par yah nahin kaha ki vah kab tak cricket maidan par vaapasi karenge
 He made it clear that he was avoiding making a hasty retreat
 unhone kaha, maine vastav main iske liye samaysima tay nahin kii he, lekin mujhe yah dekhnaa hoga ki meraa sharir kaisaa he or main maidan par kitna jaldi aa saktaa hum
 Actually i am not in a hurry and i do not want to return to fitness of 75 percent
 yuvaraj ne kaha, isamen chah maheene yaa phir do maheene kaa samay lag saktaa he
 So, i do not know
 lekin jis din main khud ko shat-pratishat feet paaungaa, main jarur vaapasi karuunga
 Yuvraj is also known for hitting six sixes in an over from Stuart Broad in the 2007 ICC World Twenty20 Championship
 unhone sanket die ki vah agle twanti-20 vishwa cap ke liye uplabdh rah sakate hai

 tab tak mujhe vaapasi kerani chahie
 Yuvraj also talked about the emotional battle against cancer
 unhone kaha, mujh jaise vyakti, jo ki chah se saat ghante abhyaas karata he or athlete kii tarah hameshaa daudta rahata he, uske liye shuru main yah sweekaar karnaa mushkil tha ki main is tarah kii beemaari se grast ho saktaa hum
 It took me a long time to accept it, but later i accepted it
 main jaanata tha ki mujhe pareshaani he or mujhe iskaa nibatara karnaa he

 indianapolis main college kaa ek chaatr mujhe dekhne ke liye aayaa or mujhe laga ki maano main bharat main hum
 i would like to thank everyone for this support
 main chemotherapy se gujara hum, jo ki kisi ke liye bhi mushkil hota he, lekin duaon or pyaar ke kaaran main isse vaapasi kar paaya

 His Sherwani was a work of art realized in a fabulous geometric Vasli pattern
 The inner kurta had self-tailoring and gota details with intricately embroidered Zardozi borders

 Mothers often come to Abu Sandeep with a picture of this ensemble, wanting their sons to wear an identical Sherwani for their big day

 lekin police se poochtacha ke dauraan sharma ne sweekaar kiya ki usne ek-do nahin balki 21 logon kii hatya kii he
